<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&nbsp;1.01.
Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July&nbsp;8,
2006, Kraft Foods International,&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;KFI&#148;) and Nabisco Euro Holdings
Ltd. (&#147;NEH&#148;), wholly owned subsidiaries of Kraft Foods Inc. (&#147;Kraft&#148;), entered
into an Agreement Relating to United Biscuits Southern Europe (the &#147;Agreement&#148;)
with United Biscuits Group (Investments) Limited, Deluxestar Limited, UB
Overseas Limited and UB Investments (Netherlands) B.V. (collectively, &#147;UB&#148;),
pursuant to which NEH will (i)&nbsp;acquire the Spanish and Portuguese
operations of UB and (ii)&nbsp;will regain the rights to all Nabisco trademarks
in the European Union, Eastern Europe, the Middle East and Africa which are
currently licensed to UB (collectively, the &#147;Business&#148;). This transaction (the &#147;Transaction&#148;)
is valued at approximately $1.070 billion on a debt-free cash-free basis.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Transaction
will be accomplished by UB transferring to NEH, in exchange for the redemption
of approximately $522 million of UB securities owned by NEH, a subsidiary that
holds the necessary rights and assets to conduct the Business. At completion of
the Transaction (&#147;Completion&#148;), the Business will have approximately $548
million of indebtedness that shall remain outstanding after completion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With effect from
Completion, KFI has waived all of its rights under a shareholders agreement in
relation to UB. KFI has guaranteed all of the obligations of NEH under the
Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The closing of the
Transaction is subject to various conditions and is currently expected to occur
in the third quarter of 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The foregoing
description of the Agreement is qualified in its entirety by reference to the
complete terms and conditions of the Agreement, which is attached as Exhibit&nbsp;10.1
to this Current Report on Form 8-K.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July&nbsp;10,
2006, Kraft issued a press release announcing the Transaction, a copy of which
is attached as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 to this Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&nbsp;9.01.
Financial Statements and Exhibits.</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(6)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">KRAFT FOODS INTERNATIONAL, INC.</font></b>, a company incorporated in
the State of Delaware and having its principal offices at Three Lakes Drive,
Northfield, Illinois, 60093, USA (<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">KFI</font></b>).</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">RECITALS:</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(A)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>United
Biscuits Iberia S.L. is a private company incorporated in Spain with registered
number B-80662950 (<b><font style="font-weight:bold;">UB&nbsp;Iberia</font></b>).
Certain details of UB Iberia and the UBSE Subsidiaries are set out in Schedule
1.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(B)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
parties intend to effect the Reorganisation prior to Completion whereby UB
Iberia will become a subsidiary of New Iberia.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(C)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>NEH
wishes to acquire the shares in New Iberia in redemption of the Discounted
Securities on the terms and subject to the conditions set out in this agreement.
The parties intend that, following Completion, the UBSE Group will hold such
rights and assets as are necessary to conduct the Business and, as between the
UB Group and the UBSE Group, other than as set out in the Transaction
Documents, all rights to the Merola Marks.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(D)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>KFI
is the holding company of NEH and is willing to guarantee the obligations of
NEH under this agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(E)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>UBGI
is the holding company of Deluxestar, UB Overseas and UB Investments and is
willing to guarantee the obligations of those parties under this agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">IT IS AGREED</font></b> as follows:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">INTERPRETATION</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In
addition to terms defined elsewhere in this agreement, the definitions and
other provisions in Schedule 7 apply throughout this agreement, unless the
contrary intention appears.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In
this agreement, unless the contrary intention appears, a reference to a clause,
sub-clause&nbsp;or Schedule is a reference to a clause, sub-clause&nbsp;or
Schedule of or to this agreement. The Schedules form part of this agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
headings in this agreement do not affect its interpretation.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">REDEMPTION</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Subject
to the Conditions being satisfied, at Completion Deluxestar shall transfer the
New Iberia Shares to NEH in redemption of the Discounted Securities.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
New Iberia Shares shall be transferred with full title guarantee free from
Encumbrances and together with all rights and benefits attaching to them.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">CONDITIONS PRECEDENT</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
acquisition of the New Iberia Shares in redemption of the Discounted Securities
is conditional on:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
UB Parties obtaining all of the consents requested in the Form&nbsp;of Waiver
Request Letter substantially in the Agreed Form&nbsp;(the <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Bank Consent
Condition</font></b>); and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>completion
of the Reorganisation (the <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Reorganisation Condition</font></b>).</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
UB Parties shall send the Form&nbsp;of Waiver Request Letter within 2 Business
Days following the date of this agreement and will use all reasonable
endeavours to procure (so far as they are able to procure) that the Bank
Consent Condition is satisfied on or before 8 September&nbsp;2006 (the <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Long Stop Date</font></b>) including, but not limited to, putting in
place and making use of a back-stop facility to replace non-consenting Lenders
accounting for up to one-third of the total amount outstanding under the Senior
Facilities Agreement.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
the Bank Consent Condition is not satisfied on or before the Long Stop Date:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>except
for this sub-clause, clauses 1, 3.8, 15, 16, 17, 18, 19, 20, 22 and 23 and the
provisions of Schedule 7, all the provisions of this agreement shall lapse and
cease to have effect; and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>neither
the lapsing of those provisions nor their ceasing to have effect shall affect
any accrued rights or liabilities of any party in respect of damages for
non-performance of any obligation falling due for performance prior to such
lapse and cessation.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Following
the date of this agreement, UBGI shall procure that the relevant members of the
UB Group and New Iberia shall observe and perform those provisions of Part&nbsp;1
of Schedule 2 as are expressed to be observed and performed by them at the
times and on the terms set out in Part&nbsp;1 of Schedule 2 provided that:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.6</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If

shall be provided to New Iberia:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>on
terms no more onerous (taken as a whole) to New Iberia than the Loan
Documentation; and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>at

of Schedule 2 have been satisfied or completed; and (ii)&nbsp;the first
Business Day on which the Bank Consent Condition is satisfied.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.7</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>UBGI
shall procure that the UB Parties (including, for the purposes of this clause
3.7, New Iberia) take such actions and sign all such documents as may
reasonably be required to:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>ensure
that the New Iberia Loan Amount is drawn down by New Iberia in accordance with
the terms set out in the Loan Documentation (or such other terms on which the
New Iberia Loan Amount may otherwise be provided pursuant to clause 3.6); and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>allow
KFI to comply with its obligations under clause 3.6.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.8</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
Completion does not take place, KFI undertakes to UBGI that it shall pay to
UBGI (as trustee for New Iberia) on a &#163; for &#163; after tax basis an amount in
respect of any costs, expenses or liabilities which may be incurred by New
Iberia pursuant to the Loan Documentation or any other documentation pursuant
to which the New Iberia Loan Amount may be made available to New Iberia
pursuant to clause 3.6, whether or not such funds are in fact drawn down,
provided that:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>if
the funds have been drawn down, only to the extent that such costs, expenses or
liabilities exceed the New Iberia Loan Amount; and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>KFI
shall have no liability under this clause 3.8 if Completion has not taken place
as a result of a breach by any UB Party or New Iberia of its obligations under
this agreement or if this agreement is terminated pursuant to clause 3.11.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.9</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Without
prejudice to the general provisions of Schedule 3 and except with the prior
written consent of KFI, UBGI will ensure that no member of the Wider UB Group
takes any action which is inconsistent with, or which might prevent or delay,
implementation of the Reorganisation.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>except

UB Parties warrant to the Kraft Parties that the Pre-Completion Warranties are
true, accurate and not misleading at the date of this agreement. KFI may
terminate this agreement by notice in writing to UBGI if, at any time between
the date of this agreement and Completion, the Kraft Parties become aware of a
fact or circumstance (other than a Disclosed Fact) which:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>would,
or might reasonably be expected to, cause any of the Pre-Completion Warranties
to be untrue, inaccurate or misleading; and</p>

applies, would reduce:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 108.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
EBITDA of the Business by &#163;5 million on an annualised basis; or</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 108.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.12</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Termination

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.13</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">5.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">COMPLETION</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Completion

shall not be obliged to complete the acquisition of any of the New Iberia

acquisition of all the New Iberia Shares is completed simultaneously.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Deluxestar

provisions of Schedule&nbsp;7, all the provisions of this agreement shall lapse
and cease to have effect; and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>neither
the lapsing of those provisions nor their ceasing to have effect shall affect
any accrued rights or liabilities of any party in respect of damages for
non-performance of any obligation falling due for performance prior to such
lapse and cessation.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">6.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">POST-COMPLETION COVENANTS</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>As
soon as reasonably practicable (and, in any event, within 15 Business Days)
after Completion, NEH shall file with the relevant commercial registry a
notarial deed of change of corporate name in respect of the change of name of
each of UB Iberia, Galletas UB and Postres UB (and shall file with the relevant
authority or commercial registry in Portugal any similar document applicable to
Portugal in respect of the change of name of UB Portugal) to a name which does
not include the word &#147;United Biscuits&#148;, &#147;UB&#148; or any name, which is the same as
or similar to, or is likely to be confused or associated with, the name of a
member of the UB Group. NEH shall provide a copy of the notarial deeds of
change of corporate name to UB&#146;s Solicitors at the same time that such deeds
are filed with the relevant commercial registry (or similar authority in
Portugal) and will notify UB&#146;s Solicitors following the registration of each
change of name.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>With
effect from Completion, NEH shall procure that, save as expressly provided in
the Transitional Services Agreement, the Supply Agreements, the Intellectual
Property Deed and the Licence Agreements, no UBSE Group Company and no member
of the Kraft Group:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>after
the expiry of 12 months from the date of Completion uses or displays (including
on or in its business stationery, documents, signs, promotional materials or
website) any name, mark or logo which is the same as or similar to, or is
likely to be confused or associated with, any name, mark or logo of a member of
the UB Group; or</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>represents
that the UB Parties or any other member of the UB Group retains any connection
with the UBSE Group Companies or any other member of the Kraft Group.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">LOANS AND GUARANTEES</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Deluxestar
shall procure that on Completion all indebtedness owing immediately before
Completion from any member of the UB Group to any UBSE Group Company (other
than </p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Deluxestar

against all liabilities under those guarantees and indemnities.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Sub-clause

consent, against Deluxestar under the Contracts (Rights of Third Parties) Act
1999. The provisions of sub-clause&nbsp;7.3 may be varied by agreement between
Deluxestar and NEH (and NEH may also release or compromise in whole or in part
any liability in respect of rights or claims contemplated by sub-clause&nbsp;7.3)
without the consent of any other member of the UBSE&nbsp;Group.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">8.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">WRONG POCKETS</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In
this clause 8:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">UB Group</font></b> means UBGI and each of its subsidiaries at
Completion and each of its subsidiaries from time to time (other than the UBSE&nbsp;Group
Companies);</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Required Asset</font></b> means an asset which relates primarily to the
business of a member of the UB Group; and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Missing Asset</font></b> means any asset which relates primarily to the
Business other than any tangible assets of, or employees engaged in, the
business of the UB Group which consists of export sales of products by members
of the UB Group which do not form part of the United Biscuits Southern Europe
business unit.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Without
prejudice to the terms of the Intellectual Property Deed or the Licence
Agreements, if after Completion any UBSE Group Company holds or owns any
Required Asset, NEH shall be deemed to hold the Required Asset(s)&nbsp;on trust
and as bailee for UBGI (for itself or on behalf of the relevant member of the
UB Group) and NEH shall, at UBGI&#146;s request, as soon as practicable and on terms
that no consideration is provided by any person for such transfer, use all
reasonable endeavours to:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>execute
all such deeds or documents as may be necessary for the purpose of transferring
(free of any lien, charge or encumbrance created after Completion) the relevant
interest in such Required Asset(s)&nbsp;to UBGI or as it may direct; and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>do
or procure to be done at UBGI&#146;s cost all such further reasonable acts or things
and procure the execution of all such other documents as UBGI (for itself or on
behalf of any member(s)&nbsp;of the UB Group) may reasonably request in order
to and for the </p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>NEH
shall notify UBGI promptly upon it coming to NEH&#146;s attention that:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>any

Group Company; or</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>any
Missing Asset(s)&nbsp;are in the possession or control of a member of the UB
Group.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Without

Agreements, if after Completion any member of the UB Group holds or owns any
Missing Asset, UBGI or that member of the UB Group as the case may be shall be
deemed to hold the Missing Asset(s)&nbsp;on trust and as bailee for NEH (for
itself and as trustee on behalf of the relevant UBSE Group Company), and UBGI
or that member of the UB Group as the case may be shall, at NEH&#146;s request, as
soon as practicable and on terms that no consideration is provided by any
person for such transfer, use all reasonable endeavours to:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 70.0pt;text-indent:-34.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>execute

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 70.0pt;text-indent:-34.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>do

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.5</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>UBGI
shall notify NEH promptly upon it coming to UBGI&#146;s&#160; attention that:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>any
Missing Asset(s)&nbsp;are in the possession or control of a member of the UB
Group; or</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>any
Required Asset(s)&nbsp;are in the possession or control of a UBSE Group
Company.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">9.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">TAX MATTERS</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
transfer of the New Iberia Shares in redemption of the Discounted Securities
pursuant to this agreement will be treated as a distribution in liquidation of
NEH&#146;s partnership interest in Deluxestar, within the meaning of Section&nbsp;732(b)&nbsp;of
the United States Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended, for all United
States federal income tax purposes.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:2.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>With
effect from the date of this agreement, UBGI shall procure that if any of the
shares in any member of the UB&nbsp;Group are to be sold or otherwise
transferred for United States federal income tax purposes prior to 31&nbsp;December&nbsp;2006,
all reasonable steps will be taken in consultation with, for a reasonable
period of time and provided such consultation does not prejudice the sale or
transfer of any such shares, and at the reasonable out of pocket expense of,
KFI with the objective that such sale or transfer is treated as a sale or
transfer of the assets of such member or will not result in any taxable gain
for a member of the Kraft Group for United States Federal income tax purposes.</p>

<div>
 <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">10.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;text-transform:none;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">WARRANTS TO SUBSCRIBE FOR SHARES IN UBGI</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">KFI warrants to UBGI that:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it is the legal and beneficial owner of the Warrants;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it is the only person who is entitled to exercise or enforce any
subscription rights or any other rights which the Warrant Instrument provides
may be exercised or enforced by a holder of Warrants; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it has not assigned, disposed of or otherwise transferred to any person
any of its Warrants or any interest in any of the Warrants or any rights
arising under or in relation to the Warrants or the Warrant Instrument.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each of the warranties contained in clause 10.1 will be deemed to be
repeated immediately before Completion.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With effect from Completion KFI:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">agrees that any and all subscription rights which it has or may have
pursuant to the Warrants or the Warrant Instrument shall lapse;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">agrees that it shall not retain any rights to enforce any subscription
rights under the Warrants;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">agrees that UBGI and every other member of the UB Group is irrevocably
released from any and all obligations and liabilities it has or may have to it
or any other member of the Kraft Group under the Warrants or the Warrant
Instrument; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">irrevocably waives, releases and discharges, to the fullest extent
permitted by law, any and all claims (including, without limitation,
cross-claims, counterclaims, rights of set-off and recoupment), causes of
action, demands, suits, costs, expenses and damages that it has or may have
arising under or relating to the Warrants or the Warrant Instrument against
UBGI, or any other member of the UB Group, or any of their respective
directors, officers, employees or advisers.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If any provision of the Warrant Instrument conflicts with the provisions
of this clause, this clause shall prevail.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">11.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;text-transform:none;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">UB WARRANTIES</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each of the UB Parties warrants to the Kraft Parties that:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it has the requisite power and authority to execute and deliver, and to
perform its obligations under, this agreement and each of the other Transaction
Documents to which it is a party, and has taken all action necessary to
authorise such execution and delivery and the performance of such obligations;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">this agreement constitutes its legal, valid and binding obligations in
accordance with its terms;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">subject to satisfaction of the Bank Consent Condition, the execution and
delivery by it of this agreement and the performance of its obligations under
it do not and will not conflict with or constitute a default under any
provision of:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">UB Investments warrants to NEH at the date of this agreement that:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it is the full owner of the UB Iberia Shares;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it is entitled to transfer or procure the transfer of the full ownership
in the UB Iberia Shares to New Iberia in accordance with the Reorganisation;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the UB Iberia Shares constitute the whole of the share capital of UB
Iberia and are fully paid up;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">UB Iberia, or another UBSE Group Company, is the full owner of the whole

Subsidiaries are fully paid up;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">no person is entitled to require any UBSE Group Company to allot, issue,
transfer, redeem or repay any share capital; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">save for the Encumbrances created pursuant to the security documents
described in Part&nbsp;3 of Schedule 6, there is no Encumbrance on, over or
affecting any of the UB Iberia Shares or any of the shares in the UBSE
Subsidiaries.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.3</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Deluxestar warrants to NEH that, subject to the satisfaction of the
Reorganisation Condition, at Completion:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it will be the full owner of the New Iberia Shares;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it will be entitled to transfer or procure the transfer of the full
ownership in the New Iberia Shares on the terms and subject to the conditions
set out in this agreement;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the New Iberia Shares will constitute the whole of the share capital of
New Iberia and will be fully paid up; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">New Iberia will be the full owner of the whole share capital of UB

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">no person will be entitled to require New Iberia to allot, issue,

 <p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font face="Times New Roman">10</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
 <p style="margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"></p>


<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">save for the Encumbrances created pursuant to the security documents
described in Part&nbsp;3 of Schedule 6, there is no Encumbrance on, over or
affecting any of the New Iberia Shares or any of the shares in UB Iberia or the
UBSE Subsidiaries.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.4</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each of the Title Warranties will be deemed to be repeated immediately
before Completion.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.5</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Title Warranties and any Title Warranty Claim shall be subject to
the limitations and other provisions set out in Schedule 5.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.6</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Nothing in Schedule 5 limits or excludes any liability for fraud.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">12.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;text-transform:none;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">KRAFT WARRANTIES</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each of the Kraft Parties warrants to the UB Parties that:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">it has the requisite power and authority to execute and deliver, and to
perform its obligations under, this agreement and each of the other Transaction
Documents to which it is a party, and has taken all action necessary to
authorise such execution and delivery and the performance of such obligations;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">this agreement constitutes legal, valid and binding obligations of it in
accordance with its terms;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">subject to the satisfaction of the Bank Consent Condition, the execution
and delivery by it of this agreement and the performance of its obligations
under it do not and will not conflict with or constitute a default under any
provision of:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 108.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">any agreement or instrument to which it is a party; or</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 108.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">its constitutional documents; or</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 108.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">any law, lien, lease, order, judgment, award, injunction, decree,
ordinance or regulation or any other restriction of any kind or character by
which it is bound;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">all authorisations from, and notices or filings with, any governmental
or other authority that are necessary to enable it to execute, deliver and
perform its obligations under this agreement have been obtained or made (as the
case may be) and are in full force and effect and all conditions of each such
authorisation have been complied with; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NEH is acquiring the New Iberia Shares for itself beneficially and there
is no agreement, arrangement or understanding (whether or not of a legally
binding nature) for the New Iberia Shares or any of the shares in the other
UBSE Group Companies, or any interest in the New Iberia Shares or in any of the
shares in the other UBSE Group Companies, to be sold, transferred or otherwise
disposed to, or held for the benefit of, any person other than NEH or another
member of the Kraft Group.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">12.2</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each of the warranties contained in clause 12.1 will be deemed to be
repeated immediately before Completion.</font></p>
