<p style="line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;">SCHEDULE 6</font></b></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">COMPLETION</font></b></p>

<p style="line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;text-transform:none;">PART&nbsp;1</font></b></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">UB
PARTIES&#146; OBLIGATIONS</font></b></p>

<p style="line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At Completion:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Deluxestar shall appear (by means of an attorney duly empowered) with
NEH before a Spanish Notary Public to sign a public document evidencing the
transfer of the New Iberia Shares to NEH;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Deluxestar shall deliver to NEH:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the original Public Deed of transfer of New Iberia Shares, evidencing
ownership over the shares by Deluxestar;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the Book of Shareholders of New Iberia duly reflecting NEH as the holder
of the New Iberia Shares;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">duly executed letters of resignation in the Agreed Form&nbsp;for each of
Mark Oldham and Susan Furst in respect of their resignations as directors of UB
Iberia;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">subject to being provided with a duly completed copy of the same, a copy
of the properly executed US tax election on Form&nbsp;8832 to treat New Iberia
as a corporation for US tax purposes signed by UB Investments; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(v)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a list of all bank accounts and safety deposit boxes held by a UBSE
Group Company, in each case showing the individuals who are entitled to sign on
such account or access such box.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">UBGI shall deliver to KFI:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">duly executed counterparts of the Transitional Services Agreement, the
Supply Agreements, the Intellectual Property Deed and the Licence Agreements;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">duly executed deeds of release of a share pledge agreement (<i><font style="font-style:italic;">p&#243;liza de cancelaci&#243;n de prenda de participaciones socials</font></i>)
or notarial deeds of cancellation of mortgage (<i><font style="font-style:italic;">escritura
p&#250;blica de cancelaci&#243;n de hipoteca inmobiliaria</font></i>) (as applicable) in
respect of each security document listed in Part&nbsp;3 of this Schedule 6;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">subject to being provided with a duly completed copy of the same, a copy
of the properly executed US tax election on Form&nbsp;8832 referenced in Step
3&#160; of Schedule 2 signed by UB
Investments;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">copies of the executed Reorganisation documents in the Agreed Form&nbsp;referred
to in Schedule 2.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Deluxestar shall ensure that at Completion a meeting of the board of
directors of UB Iberia is held at which the directors:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">appoint persons nominated by NEH to UBGI at least 10 Business Days prior
to Completion as directors and auditors of UB Iberia with effect from the end
of the meeting;</font></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;text-align:center;text-transform:uppercase;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;text-transform:none;">NEH&#146;S
OBLIGATIONS</font></b></p>

<p style="line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At Completion NEH shall:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">deliver to UBGI the Discounted Securities Extraordinary Resolution in
the Agreed Form, duly executed by NEH as the sole holder of the Discounted
Securities, consenting to the redemption of all the Discounted Securities in
exchange for the transfer of the New Iberia Shares;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">deliver to UBGI duly executed counterparts of the Transitional Services
Agreement, the Supply Agreements, the Intellectual Property Deed and the
Licence Agreements; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">deliver to UBGI, for cancellation, the certificate representing the
Warrants, or an express indemnity;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">deliver to UBGI, for cancellation, the certificate representing the
Discounted Securities, or an express indemnity;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">deliver to UBGI duly executed letters of resignation as directors or
observers of UBGI in the Agreed Form&nbsp;for each of Robert Bradish, Thomas
Dillon, Bernd Dreymueller, Jim McNasby and Linda Hefner;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">procure that New Iberia shall pay the New Iberia Loan Amount, together
with any accrued interest to the UB Account in immediately available funds for
same day value in discharge of its obligation to pay deferred consideration
pursuant to the agreement referred to in Step 8 of Schedule 2; and</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NEH shall observe and perform its obligations under clause 7.2 by

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In this agreement:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Accounts
Date</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> means 31 May&nbsp;2006;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Affiliate
</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">means, in relation to a person, any other
person, directly or indirectly, controlling or controlled by or under common
control with that person and for the purposes of this definition control when
used with respect to any person means power to direct the management and
policies of such person, directly or indirectly, whether through the ownership
of voting securities, by contract or otherwise;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Agreed Form&nbsp;</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">means, in relation to any document, the form of that document which has

Solicitors or otherwise by or on behalf of Deluxestar and NEH with such changes
as Deluxestar and NEH may agree in writing before Completion;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Balance
Sheet</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> means the consolidated balance sheet of the

Consent Condition </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">has the meaning ascribed to
it in clause 3.1(a);</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Reference
Amount</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> means the Initial Amount plus the Interest
Amount;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Reorganisation
</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">means the reorganisation described in Schedule
2 and to be implemented in accordance with clauses 3.4 and 3.5;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Restricted
Cash</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> means any cash held by a UBSE Group Company
which is not capable of being lawfully spent, distributed, loaned or released
by such UBSE Group Company from the jurisdiction in which it is situated
without deduction or withholding or additional cost (other than the costs of
transfer from a bank account incurred the ordinary course), or which is
otherwise committed (including without limitation any cash held in respect of
or securing rent deposits, in respect of UBSE Group employee withholding taxes
or any other cash held as collateral in respect of obligations of any party);</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Senior
Facilities Agreement</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> means the senior facilities
agreement dated 19 December&nbsp;1999 between, among others, UBGI as Parent,
the Lenders (as defined therein) and Deutsche Bank AG London as Agent (as
varied, supplemented or amended from time to time);</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Shareholders
Agreement</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> means the shareholders

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">subsidiary</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> means a subsidiary for the purposes of the Companies Act 1985;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Supply

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Title

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">UB

<p style="line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">a
person shall be deemed to be <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">connected</font></b> with
another if that person is connected with another within the meaning of section
839 of the Taxes Act 1988.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In this agreement any reference, express or implied, to an enactment
(which includes any legislation in any jurisdiction) includes:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">that enactment as amended, extended or applied by or under any other

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">any enactment which that enactment re-enacts (with or without

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">any subordinate legislation made (before or after signature of this

enactment which it re-enacts as described in subparagraph (b),</font></p>

<p style="line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">except
to the extent that any legislation or subordinate legislation made or enacted
after the date of this agreement would create or increase the liability of

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;line-height:13.0pt;margin:12.0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">words denoting persons include bodies corporate and unincorporated

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:12.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 3.75pt 12.0pt 0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">KRAFT FOODS EXTENDS LEADERSHIP IN BISCUITS THROUGH<br>
UNITED BISCUITS ACQUISITION IN IBERIA; RECLAIMS RIGHTS<br>
TO NABISCO TRADEMARKS IN MAJOR MARKETS</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 3.75pt 12.0pt 0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NORTHFIELD, IL, July&nbsp;10,
2006 &#151; Kraft Foods Inc. (NYSE: KFT), a global leader in branded foods and
beverages, announced today that it will acquire the Spanish and Portuguese
operations of United Biscuits (UB). The agreement also returns to Kraft the
rights to all Nabisco trademarks, including <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Oreo </font></i>and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Ritz</font></i>, in the European Union, Eastern Europe, the Middle East
and Africa.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 3.75pt 12.0pt 0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This transaction expands
Kraft&#146;s global leadership in biscuits and provides a platform to accelerate
growth in this key category through innovation and distribution gains across established
and developing markets.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">In addition to the Nabisco
trademarks, the UB operations in Spain and Portugal include leading </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">local biscuit brands, <font style="background:white;">such
as <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Fontaneda</font></i>, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Filipinos</font></i>,<i><font style="font-style:italic;"> Artiach, Chiquil&#237;n </font></i>and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Triunfo</font></i></font>,
as well as the leading dry dessert business in Iberia, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Royal</font></i>.
The deal also includes UB&#146;s Iberian canned meat, tomato, and fruit juice
businesses under the well-known brand names <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Apis</font></i> and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Fruco</font></i> as well as all seven UB manufacturing facilities and
1,300 employees in Iberia. Together, these Iberian-based businesses generated net
revenues of approximately $400 million in 2005.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Hugh Roberts, President, Kraft International
Commercial, said, &#147;We are delighted to be significantly expanding the global
scope of our Nabisco biscuit brands by recovering the licenses UB has held
since 2000. With our broader portfolio of strong trademarks, we look to achieve
even faster growth in this key category.<font style="background:white;">&#148;</font></font></p>

<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\glopez\06-16086-1\task1220080\16086-1-ma.htm',USER='glopeza',CD='Jul 12 23:18 2006' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
 <p align="right" style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:right;"></p>


<p style="color:black;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Commenting on Kraft&#146;s acquisition of UB&#146;s Spanish and
Portuguese operations, Joachim Krawczyk, Group Vice President&nbsp;&amp;
President, Kraft EU Region, said,</font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;"> </font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;This deal makes us the Iberian category leader in
biscuits and dry desserts. Through this acquisition, we are getting both great
brands and great people that we are very happy to have joining the Kraft
family.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company&#146;s acquisition of UB Iberia and the Nabisco trademark rights for the
identified markets is valued at $1,070 million, subject to certain adjustments
at closing. The acquisition is being financed by the assumption of approximately
$548 million of debt issued by the acquired business immediately prior to the
acquisition, as well as $522 million of value for the redemption of Kraft&#146;s
outstanding investment in UB, primarily deep discount securities. This
redemption will result in the recognition of a non-cash, pre-tax gain of
approximately $243 million. Excluding the impact of the one-time gain, the
transaction is expected to be approximately 2 cents accretive to earnings per
share during the first twelve months of ownership.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
transaction is expected to close in the third quarter. After closing, Kraft
will no longer have any interest in United Biscuits or any of its affiliates.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Kraft Foods (NYSE:KFT)
is the world&#146;s second-largest food and beverage company. For more than 100
years, we&#146;ve helped people around the world eat and live better. Millions of
times a day, in more than 150 countries, consumers reach for their favorite
Kraft brands including <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Kraft</font></i> cheeses
and dinners, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Jacobs, Gevalia</font></i> and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Maxwell House</font></i> coffees, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Oscar Mayer</font></i>
meats, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">DiGiorno</font></i> pizzas, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Oreo</font></i> cookies, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Ritz</font></i><b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>crackers and chips,
<i><font style="font-style:italic;">Philadelphia</font></i><b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>cream
cheese, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Milka</font></i> and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">C&#244;te d&#146;Or</font></i>
chocolates, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Honey Bunches of Oats</font></i><b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>cereals, <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Good</font></i><b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b><i><font style="font-style:italic;">Seasons</font></i> salad
dressings and <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Tang</font></i><b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>refreshment
beverages. Consumers are also adding new products like </font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Tassimo</font></i>,<b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b><i><font style="font-style:italic;">South Beach Diet</font></i><b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>and our growing range of better-for-you <i><font style="font-style:italic;">Sensible Solution</font></i><b><font style="font-weight:bold;"> </font></b>options to
their shopping baskets, continually expanding their list of Kraft favorites.</p>

<p style="color:windowtext;line-height:normal;margin:0pt -32.4pt 12.0pt 0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For more information on

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;line-height:150%;margin:0pt -32.4pt 12.0pt 0pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;line-height:150%;"># # #</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></u></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:20.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release contains projections of future
results and other forward-looking statements. One can identify these
forward-looking statements by use of words such as &#147;strategy,&#148; &#147;expects,&#148; &#147;plans,&#148;
&#147;anticipates,&#148; &#147;believes,&#148; &#147;will,&#148; &#147;continues,&#148; &#147;estimates,&#148; &#147;intends,&#148; &#147;projects,&#148;
&#147;goals,&#148; &#147;targets&#148; and other words of similar meaning. One can also identify
them by the fact that they do not relate strictly to historical or current
facts. These statements are based on the Company&#146;s current assumptions and
estimates and are subject to risks and uncertainties. In connection with the &#147;safe
harbor&#148; provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, the
Company is hereby identifying important factors that could cause actual results
and outcomes to differ materially from those contained in any forward-looking
statement made by or on behalf of the Company. These factors include: (a)&nbsp;the
effect on the Company of competition in its markets, changes in consumer
preferences and demand for its products, including diet trends, changing prices
for its raw materials and local economic and market conditions; (b)&nbsp;the
Company&#146;s continued ability to promote brand equity successfully, to anticipate
and respond to new consumer trends, to develop new products and markets, to
broaden brand portfolios, to compete effectively with lower priced products in
a consolidating environment at the retail and manufacturing levels and to
improve productivity; (c)&nbsp;the Company&#146;s ability to consummate and
successfully integrate acquisitions and to realize the cost savings and
improved asset utilization contemplated by its restructuring program; (d)&nbsp;the
impact of gains or losses, or lost operating income, from the sale of
businesses that are less of a strategic fit within the Company&#146;s portfolio; (e)&nbsp;the
effects of foreign economies, changes in tax requirements and currency
movements; (f)&nbsp;fluctuations in levels of customer inventories and credit
and other business risks related to the operations of the Company&#146;s customers; (g)&nbsp;the
Company&#146;s access to credit markets, borrowing costs and credit ratings, which
may in turn be influenced by the credit ratings of Altria Group,&nbsp;Inc.; (h)&nbsp;the
Company&#146;s benefit expense, which is subject to the investment performance of
pension plan assets, interest rates and cost increases for medical benefits
offered to employees and retirees; (i)&nbsp;the impact of recalls if products
become adulterated or misbranded, liability if product consumption causes
injury, ingredient disclosure and labeling laws and regulations, potential
claims relating to false or deceptive advertising under consumer protection or
other laws and the possibility that consumers could lose confidence in the
safety and quality of certain food products; (j)&nbsp;consumer concerns
regarding genetically modified organisms and the health implications of obesity
and trans-fatty acids; and (k)&nbsp;potential short-term volatility in
the trading volume and market </font></p>
